```javascript
test("ููฺฏุงู ุฏุฑุฎูุงุณุช ุงุฏููุ ูุทูุฆู ุดูุฏ ฺฉู ุฏุฑ ูุชุงุฌ ููุท ูุฏุฑุงู ุณูุงุฑุด ุฏุงุฏู ุดุฏู ูุณุชูุฏ", () => {
  //ุจุง ูุฑุถ ุงูฺฉู ูุง ุฏู ุงุฏูู "admin1"ุ "admin2" ู "user1" ุฑุง ุจู ุงูุฌุง ุงุถุงูู ฺฉุฑุฏู ุงู.
  const allAdmins = getUsers({ adminOnly: true });

  let admin1Found,
    adming2Found = false;

  allAdmins.forEach(aSingleUser => {
    if (aSingleUser === "user1") {
      assert.notEqual(aSingleUser, "user1", "A user was found and not admin");
    }
    if (aSingleUser === "admin1") {
      admin1Found = true;
    }
    if (aSingleUser === "admin2") {
      admin2Found = true;
    }
  });

  if (!admin1Found || !admin2Found) {
    throw new Error("Not all admins were returned");
  }
});
```

### :clap: ูุซุงู ุฏุฑุณุช: ูุฑูุฑ ุชุณุช ุงุนูุงู ุฒุฑ ฺฉ ูุณู ุงุณุช

```javascript
  //ุงู ูุชุฐ ููุท ุฏุฑ ุฏุงุฎู ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ู ุดูุฏ
```

## โช ๏ธ ๏ธ1.5 ุฏู ุจุฑุงุจุฑ ุชุณุช ููุงุณุจ ุฑุง ุงูุชุฎุงุจ ฺฉูุฏ: ุงุฒ ุชูุณุฎุฑ ุจู ููุน ุฎุฑุฏ ู ุฌุงุณูุณ ุฎูุฏุฏุงุฑ ฺฉูุฏ

### :clap: ูุชุงู ุฏุฑุณุช: ุฌุฏุง ฺฉุฑุฏู ุฌุฒุฆุงุช UI

![](https://img.shields.io/badge/๐ง%20Example%20using%20React-blue.svg "Examples with React") ![](https://img.shields.io/badge/๐ง%20Example%20using%20React%20Testing%20Library-blue.svg "Examples with react-testing-library")

```javascript
test("ููฺฏุงู ฺฉู ูุณุช ฺฉุงุฑุจุฑุงู ุจุฑุง ูุดุงู ุฏุงุฏู ููุท VIP ูพุฑฺู ฺฏุฐุงุฑ ู ุดูุฏุ ุจุงุฏ ููุท ุงุนุถุง VIP ููุงุด ุฏุงุฏู ุดูุฏ", () => {
  // ููุฏุงุฑ ุฏู ฺฉุฑุฏู

  // ุงุฌุฑุง ฺฉุฑุฏู
  const { getAllByTestId } = render(<UsersList users={allUsers} showOnlyVIP={true} />);

  // ููุงุณู ฺฉุฑุฏู - ุงุจุชุฏุง ุฏุงุฏู ูุง ุฑุง ุงุฒ UI ุงุณุชุฎุฑุงุฌ ฺฉูุฏ
  const allRenderedUsers = getAllByTestId("user").map(uiElement => uiElement.textContent);
  const allRealVIPUsers = allUsers.filter(user => user.vip).map(user => user.name);
  expect(allRenderedUsers).toEqual(allRealVIPUsers); //ุฏุงุฏู ูุง ุฑุง ุจุง ุฏุงุฏู ูุง ููุงุณู ฺฉูุฏุ ุงูุฌุง ุฑุงุจุท ฺฉุงุฑุจุฑ ูุฌูุฏ ูุฏุงุฑุฏ
});
```

### :clap: ุงูุฌุงู ุฏุฑุณุช ุขู ูุซุงู: ฺฉุงุฑ ุจู ุตูุฑุช ูุงูุน ุจูุงูู ุจุง ฺฉ ุฌุฒุก ฺฉุงููุงู ุฑูุฏุฑ ุดุฏู

![](https://img.shields.io/badge/๐ง%20Example%20using%20React-blue.svg "Examples with React") ![](https://img.shields.io/badge/๐ง%20Example%20using%20Enzyme-blue.svg "Examples with Enzyme")

```javascript
  static defaultProps = { showFilters: false };

  render() {
    return (
      <div>
        A filters panel with a button to hide/show filters
        <FiltersPanel showFilter={showFilters} title="Choose Filters" />
      </div>
    );
  }
}

//ุจุฑุง ูุซุงู ุงุฒ React & Enzyme ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ู ุดูุฏ
test("ุฑูฺฉุฑุฏ ูุงูุน ฺฏุฑุงุงูู: ููฺฏุงู ฺฉู ุจุฑุง ููุงุด ููุชุฑูุง ฺฉูฺฉ ฺฉูุฏุ ููุชุฑูุง ููุงุด ุฏุงุฏู ู ุดููุฏ", () => {
  // ููุฏุงุฑ ุฏู ฺฉุฑุฏู
  const wrapper = mount(<Calendar showFilters={false} />);

  // ุงุฌุฑุง ฺฉุฑุฏู
  wrapper.find("button").simulate("click");

  // ููุงุจุณู ฺฉุฑุฏู
  expect(wrapper.text().includes("Choose Filter"));
  // ุจู ุงู ุตูุฑุช ุงุณุช ฺฉู ฺฉุงุฑุจุฑ ุจู ุงู ุนูุตุฑ ูุฒุฏฺฉ ู ุดูุฏ: ุชูุณุท ูุชู

```

### :thumbsdown: ูุซุงู ุถุฏ ุงูฺฏู: ุชูุณุฎุฑ ูุงูุนุช ุจุง ุฑูุฏุฑ ฺฉู ุนูู


### :clap: ุงูุฌุงู ุฏุฑุณุช ูุซุงู: API E2E ฺฉู ููุท ุฒูุงู ฺฉู ุนููุงุช ููฺฏุงูโุณุงุฒ ุงูุฌุงู ุดูุฏ ุจุฑุทุฑู ูโุดูุฏ (Cypress)

### :clap: ุงูุฌุงู ุฏุฑุณุช ูุซุงู: ุขุฒูุงุด ฺฉุชุงุจุฎุงูู ุง ฺฉู ููุชุธุฑ ุนูุงุตุฑ DOM ุงุณุช

```javascript
// @testing-library/dom
test("movie title appears", async () => {
  // ุนูุตุฑ ุฏุฑ ุงุจุชุฏุง ูุฌูุฏ ูุฏุงุฑุฏ ...

  //ููุชุธุฑ ุธููุฑ ุจุงุดุฏ

    expect(getByText("the lion king")).toBeInTheDocument();

  // ููุชุธุฑ ุธุงูุฑ ุดุฏู ุจุงุดุฏ ู ุนูุตุฑ ุฑุง ุจุฑฺฏุฑุฏุงูุฏ
  const movie = await waitForElement(() => getByText("the lion king"));

```

### :thumbsdown: ูุซุงู ุถุฏ ุงูฺฏู: ฺฉุฏ ุฎูุงุจ ุณูุงุฑุด

```javascript
test("movie title appears", async () => {
  // ุนูุตุฑ ุฏุฑ ุงุจุชุฏุง ูุฌูุฏ ูุฏุงุฑุฏ ...

  // ููุทู ุงูุชุธุงุฑ ุณูุงุฑุด (ุงุญุชุงุท: ุณุงุฏูุ ุจุฏูู ูููุช ุฒูุงู)
  const interval = setInterval(() => {
    const found = getByText("the lion king");
    if (found) {
      clearInterval(interval);
      expect(getByText("the lion king")).toBeInTheDocument();
    }
  }, 100);

  // ููุชุธุฑ ุธุงูุฑ ุดุฏู ุจุงุดุฏ ู ุนูุตุฑ ุฑุง ุจุฑฺฏุฑุฏุงูุฏ
  const movie = await waitForElement(() => getByText("the lion king"));

```

## โช ๏ธ 3.5 ูุฑุงูุจ ูุญูู ุงุฑุงุฆู ูุญุชูุง ุงุฒ ุทุฑู ุดุจฺฉู ุจุงุดุฏ

![](https://img.shields.io/badge/๐ง%20Example%20using%20Google%20LightHouse-blue.svg "Examples with Lighthouse")

โ **ุงูุฌุงู ุฏุงุฏู:** ุจุฑุฎ ุงุฒ ูุงูุชูุฑูุง ูุนุงู ุฑุง ุงุนูุงู ฺฉูุฏ ฺฉู ุชุถูู ูโฺฉูุฏ ุจุงุฑฺฏุฐุงุฑ ุตูุญู ุฏุฑ ุดุจฺฉู ูุงูุน ุจููู ุดุฏู ุงุณุช - ุงู ุดุงูู ูุฑ ฺฏููู ูฺฏุฑุงู UX ูุงููุฏ ุจุงุฑฺฏุฐุงุฑ ุตูุญู ุขูุณุชู ุง ุจุณุชูโุง ฺฉูฺฺฉ ูุดุฏู ูโุดูุฏ. ุจุงุฒุงุฑ ุงุจุฒุงุฑ ุจุงุฒุฑุณ ฺฉูุชุงู ูุณุช: ุงุจุฒุงุฑูุง ุงุณุงุณ ูุงููุฏ [pingdom](https://www.pingdom.com/), AWS CloudWatch, [gcp StackDriver](https://cloud.google.com/monitoring/uptime-checks/) can be easily configured to watch whether the server is alive and response under a reasonable SLA. This only scratches the surface of what might get wrong, hence it's preferable to opt for tools that specialize in frontend (e.g. [lighthouse](https://developers.google.com/web/tools/lighthouse/), [pagespeed](https://developers.google.com/speed/pagespeed/insights/)) and perform richer analysis. The focus should be on symptoms, metrics that directly affect the UX, like page load time, [meaningful paint](https://scotch.io/courses/10-web-performance-audit-tips-for-your-next-billion-users-in-2018/fmp-first-meaningful-paint), [time until the page gets interactive (TTI)](https://calibreapp.com/blog/time-to-interactive/). On top of that, one may also watch for technical causes like ensuring the content is compressed, time to the first byte, optimize images, ensuring reasonable DOM size, SSL and many others. It's advisable to have these rich monitors both during development, as part of the CI and most important - 24x7 over the production's servers/CDN

<br/>

โ **ุฏุฑ ุบุฑ ุงู ุตูุฑุช:** ุจุงุฏ ูุงุงูุฏ ฺฉููุฏู ุจุงุดุฏ ฺฉู ูุชูุฌู ุดูุฏ ูพุณ ุงุฒ ฺูู ุฏูุช ุฒุงุฏ ุจุฑุง ุงุฌุงุฏ ฺฉ UIุ ุชุณุช ูุง ุนููฺฉุฑุฏ 100% ฺฏุฐุฑุงูุฏู ุดุฏู ู ุจุณุชู ุจูุฏ ูพฺุฏู - UX ุจู ุฏูู ูพฺฉุฑุจูุฏ ุงุดุชุจุงู CDN ูุญุดุชูุงฺฉ ู ฺฉูุฏ ุงุณุช.

### :clap: ุงูุฌุงู ุฏุฑุณุช ูุซุงู: ูุทุน ฺฉุฑุฏู ุง ุฑูฺฏุฑ ุชูุงุณโูุง API

![](https://img.shields.io/badge/๐ง%20Example%20using%20React-blue.svg "Examples with React") ![](https://img.shields.io/badge/๐ง%20Example%20using%20React%20Testing%20Library-blue.svg "Examples with react-testing-library")

```javascript
// ูุงุญุฏ ุฏุฑ ุญุงู ุขุฒูุงุด
export default function ProductsList() {
  const [products, setProducts] = useState(false);

  const fetchProducts = async () => {
    const products = await axios.get("api/products");
    setProducts(products);
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchProducts();
  }, []);

  return products ? <div>{products}</div> : <div data-test-id="no-products-message">No products</div>;
}

// ุชุณุช ฺฉุฑุฏู
test("When no products exist, show the appropriate message", () => {
  // ููุฏุงุฑ ุฏู ฺฉุฑุฏู
  nock("api")
    .get(`/products`)
    .reply(404);

  // ุงุฌุฑุง ฺฉุฑุฏู
  const { getByTestId } = render(<ProductsList />);

  // ููุงุณู ฺฉุฑุฏู
  expect(getByTestId("no-products-message")).toBeTruthy();
});
```

### :clap: ุงูุฌุงู ุฏุฑุณุช ุขู ูุซุงู: ูุจู ุงุฒ ููู ูุงุฑุฏ ุดูุฏ ู ูู ูุจู ุงุฒ ูุฑ ฺฉุฏุงู

![](https://img.shields.io/badge/๐จ%20Example%20using%20Cypress-blue.svg "Using Cypress to illustrate the idea")

```javascript
let authenticationToken;

// ูุจู ุงุฒ ุงุฌุฑุง ููู ุขุฒูุงุดุงุช ุงุชูุงู ู ุงูุชุฏ
before(() => {
  cy.request('POST', 'http://localhost:3000/login', {
    username: Cypress.env('username'),
    password: Cypress.env('password'),
  })
  .its('body')
  .then((responseFromLogin) => {
    authenticationToken = responseFromLogin.token;
  })
})

// ูุจู ุงุฒ ูุฑ ุขุฒููู ุงุชูุงู ู ุงูุชุฏ
beforeEach(setUser => {
  cy.visit('/home', () => {
    onBeforeLoad (win => {
      win.localStorage.setItem('token', JSON.stringify(authenticationToken))
    })
  })
})
```

### :clap: ุงูุฌุงู ุฏุฑุณุช ูุซุงู: ุงุณุชูุงุฏู ุงุฒ Applitools ุจุฑุง ููุงุณู ุนฺฉุณ ููุฑ ู ุณุงุฑ ูฺฺฏ ูุง ูพุดุฑูุชู

![](https://img.shields.io/badge/๐จ%20Example%20using%20AppliTools-blue.svg "Using Applitools") ![](https://img.shields.io/badge/๐จ%20Example%20using%20Cypress-blue.svg "Using Cypress to illustrate the idea")

```javascript
import * as todoPage from "../page-objects/todo-page";

describe("visual validation", () => {
  before(() => todoPage.navigate());
  beforeEach(() => cy.eyesOpen({ appName: "TAU TodoMVC" }));
  afterEach(() => cy.eyesClose());

  it("should look good", () => {
    cy.eyesCheckWindow("empty todo list");
    todoPage.addTodo("Clean room");
    todoPage.addTodo("Learn javascript");
    cy.eyesCheckWindow("two todos");
    todoPage.toggleTodo(0);
    cy.eyesCheckWindow("mark as completed");
  });
});
```
